<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> (163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">jâer</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">jār</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jērą</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yeh₁-</i>.

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:year.html>year</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage <a href = vnd.unilang:notes.html>notes</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> singular <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> normally <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:used.html>used</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:after.html>after</a> numerals <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stock.html>stock</a> phrases <a href = vnd.unilang:instead.html>instead</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> plurals <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:both.html>both</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:are.html>are</a> considered <a href = vnd.unilang:correct.html>correct</a> grammatically. <a href = vnd.unilang:thus.html>Thus</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>it</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:would.html>would</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:be.html>be</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:common.html>common</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:say.html>say</a> "<i><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geleden.html>geleden</a></i>" – <a href = vnd.unilang:many.html>many</a> years ago; <a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> "<i><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geleden.html>geleden</a></i>" – "<a href = vnd.unilang:three.html>three</a> years ago" <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> "<i><a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a></b></i>" <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> opposed <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> "<i><a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:paar.html>paar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a></i>" ("<a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:last.html>last</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:couple.html>couple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> years").
</p>

***jaguar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a> (11871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:apparently.html>Apparently</a> borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tupi_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tupi language"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> Tupi</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tpw">îagûara</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 1 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> contemporary <a href = vnd.unilang:pronunciation.html>pronunciation</a> derives <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguars.html>jaguars</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jaguar.html>jaguartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Standard_Tibetan" class="extiw" title="w:Standard Tibetan">Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Tibt mention" lang="bo">གཡག</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bo-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:g.html>g</a>.yag</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sino-Tibetan_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Sino-Tibetan languages">Proto-Sino-Tibetan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sit-pro">*g-jak ~ g-jaŋ</i>.

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:janet.html>janet</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:jeannette.html>jeannette</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jean_d%27Arc" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jean d | Arc"><a href = vnd.unilang:jean.html>Jean</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:d.html>d</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:arc.html>Arc</a></a>. Named <a href = vnd.unilang:after.html>after</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> members <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roman.html>Roman</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:catholic.html>Catholic</a> girlscouts' organisation.
